          <h2 class="date-header">
           <span>
            Friday, July 30, 2010
           </span>
          </h2>
          <div class="date-posts">
           <div class="post-outer">
            <div class="post hentry">
             <a name="8113901759033997655">
             </a>
             <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
              <a href="http://www.houseofturquoise.com/2010/07/southern-seaside-style.html">
               Southern Seaside Style
              </a>
             </h3>
             <div class="post-header-line-1">
             </div>
             <div class="post-body entry-content">
              <center>
               <img src="http://cptnrin.smugmug.com/photos/951880041_EG6z6-O.jpg"/>
               <br/>
               <img src="http://cptnrin.smugmug.com/photos/951879998_ev6NL-O.jpg"/>
               <br/>
               <img src="http://cptnrin.smugmug.com/photos/951879980_pN2KJ-O.jpg"/>
               <br/>
               <img src="http://cptnrin.smugmug.com/photos/951880096_Bqiaz-O.jpg"/>
               <br/>
               <img src="http://cptnrin.smugmug.com/photos/951880077_xFyZh-O.jpg"/>
               <br/>
               <img src="http://cptnrin.smugmug.com/photos/951880184_dyY4n-O.jpg"/>
               <br/>
               <img src="http://cptnrin.smugmug.com/photos/951880138_Z8gtD-O.jpg"/>
              </center>
              <br/>
              These folks in South Carolina don't exactly live seaside (although according to the map, they're a heck of a lot closer than I am!) but you'd never know it from their charming home designed by Jim Strickland of
              <a href="http://www.historicalconcepts.com/" target="_blank">
               Historical Concepts
              </a>
              , photographed here by Laurey W. Glenn for a feature in
              <a href="http://www.southernliving.com/home-garden/decorating/nautical-coastal-home-decor-00417000067142/page11.html" target="_blank">
               Southern Living
              </a>
              . I swear I'm hearing waves after looking at all those breezy porches! That swinging daybed?! I WANT ONE! I love all those shutters so much too, you just don't see them up here in Minnesota. We do have screened-in porches though, in fact mine is kinda like that last image. But I love how they have draperies made from waterproof sailcloth in theirs. My cute throw pillows and I could have used those during this nasty storm we had a few days ago! For more on this delightful home, head over to
              <a href="http://www.southernliving.com/home-garden/decorating/nautical-coastal-home-decor-00417000067142/" target="_blank">
               Southern Living
              </a>
              ! I hope you all have a fantastic weekend! :)
              <br/>
              <br/>
              <br/>
              <span style="font-size: 85%;">

                for even more color-themed shopping!

        <h2 class="title">
         About Me
        </h2>
        <div class="widget-content">
         <center>
          <img src="http://cptnrin.smugmug.com/photos/i-v586qpb/0/Th/i-v586qpb-Th.jpg"/>
         </center>
         Im Erin and I am obsessed with the color turquoise. I started this blog to collect inspirational photos I find of fabulous rooms that feature all of the lovely shades of my favorite color. For more turquoise fun, visit my shopping blog,
         <a href="http://www.everythingturquoise.com/" target="_blank">
          Everything Turquoise
         </a>
         . If you run into a beautiful room you know I'd love, email me:
         <a href="mailto:erin@houseofturquoise.com?subject=House%20of%20Turquoise">
          erin@houseofturquoise.com
         </a>
         !
         <br/>

function randomorder(targetarray, spacing){

var randomorder=new Array()
var the_one
var z=0
for (i=0;i&lt;targetarray.length;i++)
randomorder[i]=i

while (z&lt;targetarray.length){
the_one=Math.floor(Math.random()*targetarray.length)
if (targetarray[the_one]!="_selected!"){
document.write(targetarray[the_one]+spacing)
targetarray[the_one]="_selected!"
z++
}
}
}
